¡¡¡¡In our time it is broadly true that political writing is bad writing. Where it is not true, it will generally be found that the writer is some kind of rebel, expressing his private opinions and not a partyline.

¡¡¡¡People who write in this manner [of stale imagery and lack of precision] usually have ageneral emotional meaning they dislike one thing and want to express solidarity with another, but they are not interested in the details of what they are saying
